        }

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;

          z-index: 200;

        }

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





A page can render an autofill prompt under a Picture-in-Picture (PiP) overlay. The prompt will remain open under the PiP overlay, and selecting an autofill item using the keyboard will send data to the background page. This bypasses the fix in commit 



<span class="line"><!---->A page can render an autofill prompt under a Picture-in-Picture (PiP) overlay. The prompt will remain open under the PiP overlay, and selecting an autofill item using the keyboard will send data to the background page. This bypasses the fix in commit <!----></span>





3fb0945de5e50b8e6d2f9b0dd8a65e3f7a767b14



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/3fb0945de5e50b8e6d2f9b0dd8a65e3f7a767b14"><!---->3fb0945de5e50b8e6d2f9b0dd8a65e3f7a767b14<!----></a>





 and other checks to ensure the autofill prompt is only visible in safe conditions.



<span class="line"><!----> and other checks to ensure the autofill prompt is only visible in safe conditions.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This vulnerability has same impacts as 



<span class="line"><!---->This vulnerability has same impacts as <!----></span>





issue 1290213



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1290213" title="Security: Autofill prompt can be obscured by inactive extension-created popup, allows stealthy autofill data theft"><!---->issue 1290213<!----></a>





. The fix may be the same, since this also occurs due to the use of ShowInactive() on a window shown above the autofill prompt. But filing separately since this overlay intentionally stays above other windows and may require different considerations and fixes.



<span class="line"><!---->. The fix may be the same, since this also occurs due to the use of ShowInactive() on a window shown above the autofill prompt. But filing separately since this overlay intentionally stays above other windows and may require different considerations and fixes.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:content/browser/picture_in_picture/picture_in_picture_window_controller_impl.cc;l=92;drc=2e2b046d9f992abdf56668cb451d8e42447d290e



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:content/browser/picture_in_picture/picture_in_picture_window_controller_impl.cc;l=92;drc=2e2b046d9f992abdf56668cb451d8e42447d290e"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:content/browser/picture_in_picture/picture_in_picture_window_controller_impl.cc;l=92;drc=2e2b046d9f992abdf56668cb451d8e42447d290e<!----></a>





 calls window_->ShowInactive() on the PiP overlay window (not the page's window).



<span class="line"><!----> calls window_-&gt;ShowInactive() on the PiP overlay window (not the page's window).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The PiP overlay will only be able to obscure autofill prompts under the overlay, and at least on my Windows system, the PiP overlay consistently appears near the bottom-right of the screen. Therefore, a successful attack will only work if the window is maximized or covers the bottom-right of the screen. The PoC checks the window position and instructs the user to move or maximize the window if it's not covering the expected area.



<span class="line"><!---->The PiP overlay will only be able to obscure autofill prompts under the overlay, and at least on my Windows system, the PiP overlay consistently appears near the bottom-right of the screen. Therefore, a successful attack will only work if the window is maximized or covers the bottom-right of the screen. The PoC checks the window position and instructs the user to move or maximize the window if it's not covering the expected area.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





ADDITIONAL CONTEXT



<span class="line"><!---->ADDITIONAL CONTEXT<!----></span>



<br>





Opening the autofill prompt and selecting an autofill item are possible only via keyboard input, since the down arrow selects the autofill item on the first step, and the PiP overlay prevents any mouse interaction with the obscured autofill prompt on the second step.



<span class="line"><!---->Opening the autofill prompt and selecting an autofill item are possible only via keyboard input, since the down arrow selects the autofill item on the first step, and the PiP overlay prevents any mouse interaction with the obscured autofill prompt on the second step.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I've tested this with addresses (which includes name + email), credit cards, and single-field autofills.



<span class="line"><!---->I've tested this with addresses (which includes name + email), credit cards, and single-field autofills.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: 97.0.4692.71 Stable, 100.0.4850.3 Canary



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: 97.0.4692.71 Stable, 100.0.4850.3 Canary<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: Windows 10 Version 20H2 (Build 19042.1415)



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: Windows 10 Version 20H2 (Build 19042.1415)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->PoC for address (multiple fields):<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->Prerequisites: Have at least one address with email address in chrome://settings/addresses<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->1. Navigate to <!----></span>





https://alesandroortiz.com/security/chromium/autofill-obscured-pip.html

<br>





2. Press down arrow in keyboard.



<span class="line"><!---->2. Press down arrow in keyboard.<!----></span>



<br>





3. Press enter (or tab) in keyboard.



<span class="line"><!---->3. Press enter (or tab) in keyboard.<!----></span>



<br>





(After step 3, extension will close the PiP overlay on a delay to make PoC behavior clearer, but the delay is not needed. You can also manually close the PiP overlay.)



<span class="line"><!---->(After step 3, extension will close the PiP overlay on a delay to make PoC behavior clearer, but the delay is not needed. You can also manually close the PiP overlay.)<!----></span>

FWIW, this also occludes most other browser UI including those identified in 



<span class="line"><!---->FWIW, this also occludes most other browser UI including those identified in <!----></span>





issue 1302159



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1302159" title="Security: Extension can obscure active window with an inactive window, user can interact with sensitive UI using keyboard without being aware"><!---->issue 1302159<!----></a>





. The main limitation is the position of the PiP window being in the bottom right of the screen. However, a website can create a window with an additional user interaction in that area with the sensitive UI, or an extension can create the window without user interaction. I can develop PoCs if helpful for those other scenarios in the next week or two.



<span class="line"><!---->. The main limitation is the position of the PiP window being in the bottom right of the screen. However, a website can create a window with an additional user interaction in that area with the sensitive UI, or an extension can create the window without user interaction. I can develop PoCs if helpful for those other scenarios in the next week or two.<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.
